                                BEGIN
                                  TryOutSucc.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
                                  TryOutSucc.SETFILTER("Try-out No.", '<>%1','');

                                  TryOutSucc.SETRANGE("Try-out No.");
                                  TryOutSucc.SETFILTER("Try-out Quote",'<>%1','');

                                    TryOutCode := TryOutSucc."Try-out Quote";

                                  END;
                                END;

    { 1100525001;1;DataItem;MatHA            ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               DefineVendors;
                               DefineEstimateLine;
                               DefOANw;
                               DefineOA;
                               DefinePlant;
                               DefineSundry;
                               TmpLine.RESET;
                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, TmpLine.COUNT);
                               PrintTotalMat := FALSE;
                               TempKD := '';
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TmpLine.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TmpLine.NEXT;

                                  IF (TmpLine."Key Code1" <> TempKD) AND (TempKD = '') THEN BEGIN
                                    TmpKD.GET(TmpLine."Key Code1");
                                    LineCnt := TmpKD."Days Notify Buyer" -1;
                                    KG1 := (TmpLine.Dec2 / TmpLine.Int1);
                                    Mattotal += TmpLine.Dec1;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    IF TempKD = '' THEN BEGIN
                                      TmpKD.GET(TmpLine."Key Code1");
                                      LineCnt := TmpKD."Days Notify Buyer" - 1;
                                      Mattotal += TmpLine.Dec1;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      LineCnt := LineCnt - 1;
                                      Mattotal += TmpLine.Dec1;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  PrintTotalMat := (LineCnt = 0);

                                  IF PrintTotalMat THEN
                                    TempKD := ''
                                  ELSE
                                    TempKD := TmpLine."Key Code1";

                                  //output
                                  CASE TmpLine."Key Code1" OF
                                    '204', '205', '206' : IF UsedSalesPrice(TmpLine."Key Code1") THEN
                                        ShowOutput1MatHA := TRUE
                                      ELSE
                                        ShowOutput1MatHA := FALSE;
                                    ELSE
                                      ShowOutput1MatHA := FALSE;
                                  END;

                                  ShowOutput2MatHA := PrintTotalMat;
                                  IF ShowOutput2MatHA THEN BEGIN
                                    WithSurch := GiveTotalOpls(TmpLine."Key Code1");
                                    InclusiefSurch := GiveTotal(TmpLine."Key Code1") + WithSurch;
                                    MatOverallTot += InclusiefSurch;
                                  END;


                                  IF ShowOutput3MatHA THEN BEGIN
                                    WithSurch := GiveTotal(TmpLine."Key Code1") * KG1 / 100;
                                    InclusiefSurch := GiveTotal(TmpLine."Key Code1") + WithSurch;
                                    DekMat := MatOverallTot - Mattotal;
                                    DecPercMat := ((MatOverallTot / Mattotal) -1) * 100
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525104;2;Column;Number_MatHA       ;
               SourceExpr=MatHA.Number }

    { 1100525003;1;DataItem;OANw             ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               TmpBudgetLine2.RESET;
                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, TmpBudgetLine2.COUNT);
                               TempKD := '';
                               PrintTotalOA := FALSE;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TmpBudgetLine2.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TmpBudgetLine2.NEXT;

                                  IF TmpBudgetLine2."Project No." <> TempKD THEN BEGIN
                                    KD := TmpBudgetLine2."Project No.";
                                    KG1 := TmpBudgetLine2."Time Quantity";
                                    KD1 := TmpBudgetLine2."Project No.";
                                    TmpKD2.GET(TmpBudgetLine2."Project No.");
                                    LineCnt := TmpKD2."Days Notify Buyer" -1 ;
                                    OAtot += TmpKD2."% Labor";
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    KD := '';
                                    LineCnt := LineCnt - 1;
                                  END;

                                  PrintTotalOA := (LineCnt = 0);

                                  TempKD := TmpBudgetLine2."Project No.";

                                  //output
                                  ShowOutput4OANw := PrintTotalOA;

                                  IF ShowOutput4OANw THEN BEGIN
                                    IF KG1 <> 0 THEN
                                      WithSurch := GiveTotal2(TmpBudgetLine2."Project No.") * KG1 / 100;
                                    InclusiefSurch := GiveTotal2(TmpBudgetLine2."Project No.") + WithSurch;
                                    OAOverallTot += InclusiefSurch;
                                  END;

                                  IF ShowOutput5OANw THEN BEGIN
                                    DEKOA := OAOverallTot - OAtot;
                                    IF OAtot <> 0 THEN
                                      DecPercOA := ((OAOverallTot / OAtot) -1) * 100
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    PROCEDURE DefineVendors@1000000010();
    VAR
      TradeVendRec@1000000000 : Record 11012304;
      VendRec@1000000001 : Record 23;
    BEGIN
      TempTrVend.RESET;
      TempTrVend.DELETEALL;
      TempVend.RESET;
      TempVend.DELETEALL;
      TempVendWv.RESET;
      TempVendWv.DELETEALL;
      OATempRec.RESET;
      OATempRec.DELETEALL;
      OAWKDTempRec.RESET;
      OAWKDTempRec.DELETEALL;
      OAIMINFTempRec.RESET;
      OAIMINFTempRec.DELETEALL;
      OAIMNVTempRec.RESET;
      OAIMNVTempRec.DELETEALL;
      TmpBudgetLine.RESET;
      TmpBudgetLine.DELETEALL;
      TmpKD.RESET;
      TmpKD.DELETEALL;
      TmpBudgetLine2.RESET;
      TmpBudgetLine2.DELETEALL;
      TmpKD2.RESET;
      TmpKD2.DELETEALL;

      EstLineRAW.RESET;
      EstLineRAW.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Vendor (Trade Item)",'<>%1', '');
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER(Vendor, '=%1', '');
      IF EstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF NOT TempTrVend.GET(EstLineRAW."Vendor (Trade Item)") THEN BEGIN
            TradeVendRec.GET(EstLineRAW."Vendor (Trade Item)");
            CreateTempRec(EstLineRAW."Vendor (Trade Item)", TradeVendRec.Name);
          END;
          InsertHeadRec(EstLineRAW."Cumulative Material");
          InsertDetRec(EstLineRAW);
        UNTIL EstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EstLineRAW.SETRANGE("Vendor (Trade Item)");
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER(Vendor, '<>%1', '');
      IF EstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF NOT TempVend.GET(EstLineRAW.Vendor) THEN BEGIN
            VendRec.GET(EstLineRAW.Vendor);
            CreateTempVRec(EstLineRAW.Vendor, VendRec.Name);
          END;
          InsertHeadIRec(EstLineRAW."Cumulative Material");
          InsertDetIRec(EstLineRAW);
        UNTIL EstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Vendor (Trade Item)",'%1', '');
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER(Vendor, '%1', '');
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Cumulative Material", '<>%1',0);
      IF EstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          InsertHeadIIRec(EstLineRAW."Cumulative Material");
          InsertDetIIRec(EstLineRAW);
          WithVenDescr := EstLineRAW.Description;
        UNTIL EstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

      TempTrVend.Name := Name;
      TempTrVend.INSERT;
      TradeVendCntr += 1;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DefineOA@1000000000();
    BEGIN
      EstLineRAW.RESET;
      EstLineRAW.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Cost Object Subcontracting",'<>%1', '');
      IF EstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          EstLineRAW.CALCFIELDS("Subcontractor Name");
          CASE EstLineRAW."Cost Object Subcontracting" OF
            '300': IF EstLineRAW."Subcontractor Name" <> '' THEN
                     CreateOA(EstLineRAW.Subcontractor, EstLineRAW."Subcontractor Name", EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting")
                   ELSE
                     CreateOA('OA', EstLineRAW.Description, EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting");
            '320': IF EstLineRAW."Subcontractor Name" <> '' THEN
                     CreateOAIMINF(EstLineRAW.Subcontractor, EstLineRAW."Subcontractor Name", EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting")
                   ELSE
                     CreateOAIMINF('OA', EstLineRAW.Description, EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting");
            '340': IF EstLineRAW."Subcontractor Name" <> '' THEN
                     CreateOAIMNV(EstLineRAW.Subcontractor, EstLineRAW."Subcontractor Name", EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting")
                   ELSE
                     CreateOAIMNV('OA', EstLineRAW.Description, EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting");
            ELSE
              IF EstLineRAW."Subcontractor Name" <> '' THEN
                CreateOAWOA(EstLineRAW.Subcontractor, EstLineRAW."Subcontractor Name", EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting",
                  EstLineRAW.Description)
              ELSE
                CreateOAWOA('OA', EstLineRAW.Description, EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting",
                  EstLineRAW.Description)
            END;
        UNTIL EstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Cost Object Subcontracting",'=%1', '');
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER(Subcontractor, '<>%1', '');
      IF EstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          EstLineRAW.CALCFIELDS("Subcontractor Name");
          CreateOAWKD(EstLineRAW.Subcontractor, EstLineRAW."Subcontractor Name", EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting");
        UNTIL EstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Cost Object Subcontracting",'=%1', '');
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER(Subcontractor, '=%1', '');
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Subcontracting Price", '<>%1', 0);
      IF EstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          CreateOAWOA('OA', EstLineRAW.Description, EstLineRAW."Cumulative Subcontracting",
            EstLineRAW.Description)
        UNTIL EstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    END;

    PROCEDURE DefinePlant@1000000066();
    VAR
      PlantType@1000000000 : Record 11012551;
    BEGIN
      EstLineRAW.RESET;
      EstLineRAW.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
      EstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Plant Price",'<>%1', 0);
      IF EstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        PlantTypeCnt := 1;
        REPEAT
          CreateTempPlantType(EstLineRAW.Description, EstLineRAW."Cumulative Plant",
            EstLineRAW."Cumulative Hours (Plant)", EstLineRAW."Plant Price");
        UNTIL EstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTempPlantType@1000000071(Name@1000000001 : Text[50];Amnt@1000000002 : Decimal;hrs@1000000003 : Decimal;Price@1000000004 : Decimal);
    BEGIN
      TemPlantTypeRec.RESET;
      TemPlantTypeRec.SETRANGE(Description, Name);
      IF TemPlantTypeRec.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        TemPlantTypeRec.Weight += Amnt;
        TemPlantTypeRec."No. of Depreciation Years" += hrs;
        TemPlantTypeRec.MODIFY;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TemPlantTypeRec.INIT;
        TemPlantTypeRec.Code := STRSUBSTNO('%1',PlantTypeCnt);
        TemPlantTypeRec.Description := Name;
        TemPlantTypeRec.Weight := Amnt;
        TemPlantTypeRec."Current Price" := Price;
        TemPlantTypeRec."No. of Depreciation Years" := hrs;
        TemPlantTypeRec.INSERT;
        PlantTypeCnt += 1;
      END;

      PlantTot += Amnt;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateHrsByRate@1000000096(RateCde@1000000000 : Code[20];VAR Total@1000000001 : Decimal) totamnt : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      EstLineRAW.RESET;
      EstLineRAW.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
      EstLineRAW.SETRANGE("Rate Code", RateCde);
      IF EstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          totamnt += EstLineRAW."Cumulative Labor";
          Total += EstLineRAW."Cumulative Hours";
        UNTIL EstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DefineIndexering@1000000018() i : Integer;
    VAR
      CommentLineRec@1000000000 : Record 97;
      HeadRow@1000000001 : Integer;
      LastRow@1000000002 : Integer;
      LineFilter@1000000003 : Text[50];
    BEGIN
      TempCommentLineRec.RESET;
      TempCommentLineRec.DELETEALL;

      CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineRec."Table Name"::Estimate);
      CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("No.", Estimate."No.");
      CommentLineRec.SETFILTER(Code, 'INDEX');
      IF CommentLineRec.FINDFIRST THEN
        HeadRow := CommentLineRec."Line No.";
      CommentLineRec.SETFILTER(Code, '<>%1','');
      CommentLineRec.SETFILTER("Line No.",'>%1', HeadRow);
      IF CommentLineRec.FINDFIRST THEN
        LastRow := CommentLineRec."Line No."
      ELSE
        LastRow := 1000000000;

      CommentLineRec.RESET;
      CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineRec."Table Name"::Estimate);
      CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("No.", Estimate."No.");
      LineFilter := STRSUBSTNO('%1..%2', HeadRow + 1, LastRow - 1);
      CommentLineRec.SETFILTER("Line No.", LineFilter);
      IF CommentLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          TempCommentLineRec := CommentLineRec;
          TempCommentLineRec.INSERT;
          i += 1;
        UNTIL CommentLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DefineWinstenRisico@1000000029() i : Integer;
    VAR
      CommentLineRec@1000000000 : Record 97;

      LineFilter@1000000003 : Text[50];

        HeadRow := CommentLineRec."Line No.";
      CommentLineRec.SETFILTER(Code, '<>%1','');
      CommentLineRec.SETFILTER("Line No.",'>%1', HeadRow);
      IF CommentLineRec.FINDFIRST THEN
        LastRow := CommentLineRec."Line No."
      ELSE
        LastRow := 1000000000;

      CommentLineRec.RESET;
      CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineRec."Table Name"::Estimate);
      CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("No.", Estimate."No.");
      LineFilter := STRSUBSTNO('%1..%2', HeadRow + 1, LastRow - 1);
      CommentLineRec.SETFILTER("Line No.", LineFilter);
      IF CommentLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          TempCommentLineRec := CommentLineRec;
          TempCommentLineRec.INSERT;
          i += 1;
        UNTIL CommentLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetICodeValue@1000000013(ICode@1000000000 : Integer;Perc@1000000001 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      CASE ICode OF
        1: ArrDec[ICode] := ((((MatHandArt / 100) * Perc)));
        2: ArrDec[ICode] := ((((MatArtikel / 100) * Perc)));
        3: ArrDec[ICode] := ((((OAtot      / 100) * Perc)));
        4: ArrDec[ICode] := ((((OAIMINFtot / 100) * Perc)));
        5: ArrDec[ICode] := ((((OAIMNVtot  / 100) * Perc)));
        6: ArrDec[ICode] := ((((PlantTot   / 100) * Perc)));
        7: ArrDec[ICode] := ((((TotLoon    / 100) * Perc)));
      END;

      EXIT(ArrDec[ICode]);
    END;

    PROCEDURE "GetICodeValueW&R"@1000000064(ICode@1000000000 : Integer;Perc@1000000001 : Decimal) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      CASE ICode OF
        1: IF ArrDec[ICode] <> 0 THEN
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((MatHandArt + ArrDec[ICode]) / 100) * Perc))
           ELSE
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := (((MatHandArt / 100) * Perc));
        2: IF ArrDec[ICode] <> 0 THEN
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((MatHandArt + ArrDec[ICode]) / 100) * Perc))
           ELSE
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((MatArtikel / 100) * Perc)));
        3: IF ArrDec[ICode] <> 0 THEN
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((OAtot + ArrDec[ICode]) / 100) * Perc))
           ELSE
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((OAtot / 100) * Perc)));
        4: IF ArrDec[ICode] <> 0 THEN
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((OAIMINFtot + ArrDec[ICode]) / 100) * Perc))
           ELSE
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((OAIMINFtot / 100) * Perc)));
        5: IF ArrDec[ICode] <> 0 THEN
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((OAIMNVtot + ArrDec[ICode]) / 100) * Perc))
           ELSE
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((OAIMNVtot / 100) * Perc)));
        6: IF ArrDec[ICode] <> 0 THEN
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((PlantTot + ArrDec[ICode])  / 100) * Perc))
           ELSE
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((PlantTot / 100) * Perc)));
        7: IF ArrDec[ICode] <> 0 THEN
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((TotLoon + ArrDec[ICode]) / 100) * Perc))
           ELSE
             ArrwrDec[ICode] := ((((TotLoon  / 100) * Perc)));
      END;

      EXIT(ArrwrDec[ICode]);
    END;

    PROCEDURE DefineEstimateLine@1000000001();
    VAR
      lEstLineRAW@1000000000 : Record 11125680;
    BEGIN
      lEstLineRAW.RESET;
      lEstLineRAW.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
      lEstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Material Amount",'<>%1', 0);
      //EstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Vendor (Trade Item)",'<>%1', '');
      //EstLineRAW.SETFILTER(Vendor, '<>%1', '');
      IF lEstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF lEstLineRAW."Cost Object Material" = '' THEN
            ERROR(Text000,lEstLineRAW.FIELDCAPTION("Cost Object Material"))
          ELSE
            TryCatchTempLine(lEstLineRAW);
        UNTIL lEstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE TryCatchTempLine@1000000021(EstLineRAWLocal@1000000000 : Record 11125680);
    VAR
      VendorFilter@1000000001 : Code[20];
      EstimateRAWSurcharge@1000000002 : Record 11012236;
      Vendor@1000000003 : Record 23;
      EtimVendor@1000000004 : Record 11012304;
      VendorName@1000000005 : Text[50];
    BEGIN
      IF EstLineRAWLocal."Vendor (Trade Item)" <> '' THEN BEGIN
        VendorFilter := EstLineRAWLocal."Vendor (Trade Item)";
        EtimVendor.GET(VendorFilter);
        VendorName := EtimVendor.Name;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF EstLineRAWLocal.Vendor <> '' THEN BEGIN
          VendorFilter := EstLineRAWLocal.Vendor;
          Vendor.GET(VendorFilter);
          VendorName := Vendor.Name;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          VendorFilter := 'LEEG';
          VendorName := 'LEEG';
        END;
      END;

      TmpLine.RESET;
      IF TmpLine.GET(EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Material", VendorFilter) THEN BEGIN
        TmpLine.Dec1 += EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Material";
        TmpLine.Dec2 += EstLineRAWLocal."Surcharge % Material";
        TmpLine.Dec3 := EstLineRAWLocal."Surcharge Amount Material";
        IF EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Material" <> 0 THEN
          TmpLine.Int1 += 1;
        IF TmpKD.GET(EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Material") THEN BEGIN
          TmpKD."% Labor" += EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Material";
          TmpKD."% to B Account" += EstLineRAWLocal."Surcharge Amount Material";
          TmpKD.MODIFY;
        END;
        TmpLine.MODIFY;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TmpLine."Key Code1" := EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Material";
        TmpLine."Key Code2" := VendorFilter;
        TmpLine.Dec1 := EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Material";
        TmpLine.Dec2 := EstLineRAWLocal."Surcharge % Material";
        TmpLine.Dec3 := EstLineRAWLocal."Surcharge Amount Material";
        IF EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Material" <> 0 THEN
          TmpLine.Int1 := 1;
        TmpLine.Text1 := EstLineRAWLocal.Description;
        TmpLine.Text2 := VendorName;
        TmpLine.INSERT;
        IF TmpKD.GET(EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Material") THEN BEGIN
          TmpKD."Days Notify Buyer" += 1;
          TmpKD."% Labor" += EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Material";
          TmpKD."% to B Account" += EstLineRAWLocal."Surcharge Amount Material";
          TmpKD.MODIFY;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          TmpKD.INIT;
          TmpKD."No." := EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Material";
          TmpKD."% Labor" := EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Material";
          TmpKD."% to B Account" := EstLineRAWLocal."Surcharge Amount Material";
          TmpKD."Days Notify Buyer" := 1;
          TmpKD.INSERT;
        END;

      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GiveTotal@1000000026(costobj@1000000000 : Code[20]) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TmpKD.RESET;
      TmpKD.GET(costobj);
      EXIT(TmpKD."% Labor");
    END;

    PROCEDURE DefOANw@1000000003();
    VAR
      lEstLineRAW@1000000000 : Record 11125680;
    BEGIN
      lEstLineRAW.RESET;
      lEstLineRAW.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
      lEstLineRAW.SETFILTER("Subcontracting Amount",'<>%1', 0);
      IF lEstLineRAW.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF lEstLineRAW."Cost Object Subcontracting" = '' THEN
            ERROR(Text000,lEstLineRAW.FIELDCAPTION("Cost Object Subcontracting"))
          ELSE
            TryCatchOATempLine(lEstLineRAW);
        UNTIL lEstLineRAW.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE TryCatchOATempLine@1000000014(EstLineRAWLocal@1000000000 : Record 11125680);
    VAR
      VendorFilter@1000000001 : Code[20];
      EstimateRAWSurcharge@1000000002 : Record 11012236;
      VendorRec@1000000003 : Record 23;
      EtimVendor@1000000004 : Record 11012304;
    BEGIN
      //Project No.,Adjustment,Extension Contract,Option,Line No.
      TmpBudgetLine2.RESET;
      TmpBudgetLine2.SETRANGE("Project No.", EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Subcontracting");
      IF EstLineRAWLocal.Subcontractor <> '' THEN
        VendorFilter := EstLineRAWLocal.Subcontractor
      ELSE
        VendorFilter := ' ';

      TmpBudgetLine2.SETRANGE(Adjustment, VendorFilter);
      TmpBudgetLine2.SETRANGE("Extension Contract",'G');
      TmpBudgetLine2.SETFILTER("Line No.",'<>%1', 0);
      TmpBudgetLine2.SETRANGE(Option,'S');
      IF TmpBudgetLine2.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        TmpBudgetLine2.Amount += (EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Subcontracting");
        TmpBudgetLine2.MODIFY;
        IF TmpKD2.GET(EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Subcontracting") THEN BEGIN
          TmpKD2."% Labor" += EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Subcontracting";
          TmpKD2.MODIFY;
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TmpBudgetLine2.INIT;
        TmpBudgetLine2."Project No." := EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Subcontracting";
        TmpBudgetLine2.Adjustment := VendorFilter;
        TmpBudgetLine2."Extension Contract" := 'G';
        TmpBudgetLine2.Option := 'S';
        TmpBudgetLine2."Line No." := TmpBudgetLine2."Line No." + 10000;
        IF TmpBudgetLine2.Adjustment = '' THEN
          TmpBudgetLine2.Description := COPYSTR(EstLineRAWLocal.Description,1,50);
        IF VendorRec.GET(VendorFilter) THEN
          TmpBudgetLine2."Description 2" := VendorRec.Name;
        IF TmpBudgetLine2."Description 2" = '' THEN BEGIN
          IF EtimVendor.GET(VendorFilter) THEN
            TmpBudgetLine2."Description 2" := EtimVendor.Name;
        END;
        TmpBudgetLine2.Amount := EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Subcontracting";
        IF EstimateRAWSurcharge.GET(TmpBudgetLine2."Project No.",Estimate."No.") THEN BEGIN
          IF EstimateRAWSurcharge."Surcharge %" <> 0 THEN
            TmpBudgetLine2."Time Quantity" := EstimateRAWSurcharge."Surcharge %"
          ELSE
            TmpBudgetLine2."Time Quantity" := EstLineRAWLocal."Surcharge % Subcontracting"
        END ELSE
          TmpBudgetLine2."Time Quantity" := EstLineRAWLocal."Surcharge % Subcontracting";
        TmpBudgetLine2.INSERT;
        IF NOT TmpKD2.GET(EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Subcontracting") THEN BEGIN
          TmpKD2.INIT;
          TmpKD2."No." := EstLineRAWLocal."Cost Object Subcontracting";
          TmpKD2."% Labor" := EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Subcontracting";
          TmpKD2."Days Notify Buyer" := 1;
          TmpKD2.INSERT
        END ELSE BEGIN
          TmpKD2."% Labor" += EstLineRAWLocal."Cumulative Subcontracting";
          TmpKD2."Days Notify Buyer" += 1;
          TmpKD2.MODIFY;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GiveTotal2@1000000042(costobj@1000000000 : Code[20]) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TmpKD2.GET(costobj);
      EXIT(TmpKD2."% Labor");
    END;

    PROCEDURE GiveTotalOpls@1000000019(costobj@1000000000 : Code[20]) : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TmpKD.RESET;
      TmpKD.GET(costobj);
      EXIT(TmpKD."% to B Account");
    END;

    PROCEDURE UsedSalesPrice@1000000007(CostObj@1000000002 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      EstimateLineRec@1000000004 : Record 11125680;
      RecipeLine@1000000001 : Record 11012156;
      DiscountTermHistory@1000000003 : Record 11012312;
    BEGIN
      EstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Estimate No.", Estimate."No.");
      EstimateLineRec.SETRANGE("Cost Object Material", CostObj);
      IF EstimateLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          DiscountTermHistory.SETRANGE(Vendor, EstimateLineRec."Vendor (Trade Item)");
          DiscountTermHistory.SETRANGE("Item Code", EstimateLineRec."Trade Item");
          DiscountTermHistory.SETFILTER("Starting Date", '<=%1', TODAY);
          DiscountTermHistory.SETFILTER("Sales Price", '<>0');
          IF NOT DiscountTermHistory.ISEMPTY THEN
            EXIT(TRUE);
        UNTIL EstimateLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      EXIT(FALSE);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function


Shared offset as Integer
Shared newPage as Object
Shared currentgroup1 as Object
Shared currentgroup2 as Object
Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(NewPage as Boolean, pagenumber as Integer) as Object
  If NewPage
    offset = pagenumber - 1
  End If
  Return pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function IsNewPage(group1 as Object, group2 as Object) As Boolean
newPage = FALSE
If Not (group1 = currentgroup1)
   NewPage = TRUE
   currentgroup2 = group2
   currentgroup1 = group1
ELSE
   If Not (group2 = currentgroup2)
      NewPage = TRUE
      currentgroup2 = group2
   End If
End If
Return NewPage
End Function



Shared Data1 as Object

Public Function GetData(Num as Integer, Group as integer) as Object
if Group = 1 then
   Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1),Chr(177))))
End If
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData as Object,Group as integer)
  If Group = 1 and NewData &gt; "" Then
      Data1 = NewData
  End If
  Return True
End Function</Code>
